msg:I stayed at your hotel in Hampton by Hilton Xiamen City Plaza,China  in a multimedia room on October 2, 2023, with the hope of experiencing the high-quality service promised by the Hilton brand. However, I feel compelled to provide feedback on a series of issues I encountered during my stay, which seriously impacted my overall experience.

Firstly, I was struck by the lack of professionalism at the front desk. Upon check-in, there was no information provided about the hotel's facilities, and I was not informed about whether breakfast was included. It was only later that I discovered my room reservation included complimentary breakfast, but unfortunately, I had missed out on this amenity due to the lack of communication. This absence of information made my stay less enjoyable.

Even more frustrating was the significant odor and smoke in the room I was assigned to, which I found unbearable. To make matters worse, I discovered a cockroach in the room's bathroom, a hygiene issue that severely eroded my trust, especially considering this is a Hilton-affiliated hotel.

After I brought these issues to the attention of the front desk, they changed my room. However, the new room had extremely poor soundproofing, and I was disturbed throughout the night by the sound of children crying and activities from the adjacent room, making it very difficult for me to rest.

As a loyal Hilton customer, I am deeply disappointed by this stay. I expected to experience exceptional service and a comfortable accommodation environment at your hotel, but this experience fell far short of my expectations.

I hope that your hotel will take my complaint seriously and take appropriate steps to improve the service and maintain hygiene standards. I look forward to your response to understand how you plan to address these issues.

I wonder why such a distinctive hotel does not have a name. The architectural style is a tulou-shaped ring, and the breakfast is so rich and excellent that people want to sleep for breakfast.
surroundings:
This may be the biggest feature. The whole hotel is a hollow circular building style, like Fujian Tulou, with a sealed roof. Looking down from the upstairs, there is only a restaurant on the 2nd floor. With this style, you can definitely be served breakfast in the morning. The fragrance wakes up.
The location of the hotel is not good, but there are various business circles and scenic spots around, such as SM City Plaza and Mingfa Plaza, which are all nearby. It is a great choice to choose this hotel. It is about 3 kilometers away from the airport and about the same distance from the Science and Technology Museum. It takes less than 15 minutes by taxi. It is also very convenient to take the subway. It is just at Xiaodongshan Station on Line 3. As long as you are not too troublesome and not in a hurry, this is definitely a convenient choice for accommodation. No wonder the surrounding housing prices are 60,000+‚Ä¶
Serve:
The service is very enthusiastic. When I checked in, I wanted to add a quilt because I brought my baby. When I asked, I was very enthusiastic and told that there was no problem. The elder sister who was cleaning was also kind and enthusiastic, and she would not feel a professional smile when greeting, very sincere. It's not like many hotel cleaning aunts who seem to be very resentful, and the overall is very clean. The bathroom products are a brand that I have used before. I can't tell you. The shower gel smells like orange. I have to say that in the selection of bathroom products, domestic chain hotels really need to upgrade. The improvement of sophistication is often in these details.

The hotel's breakfast really needs special mention, it's really great. When I wake up in the morning, the first thing my baby does is open the door and look at the restaurant below, and see that someone has been busy preparing very early. There is no need to say more about clean and hygienic. The ingredients are fresh and carefully prepared, meat and vegetables are matched, there is a noodle cooking window, and there is a small table with characteristics of southern Fujian prepared five-spice rolls, peanut soup and noodle paste, the eldest sister of the fried egg He is skilled in cooking, efficient and neat in his work, and in a short time he cooked a large plate full of eggs and double-sided candy hearts. He also neatly made sandwiches, waffles, bacon, and various sausages. At first glance, he was a good housekeeper.
There are not many kinds of fruits in the fruit area, but there are watermelons that are not often eaten, which are very sweet and fresh. It is really a luxury to eat such watermelons in winter.
There are small cakes and various kinds of bread in the dessert area, and the toast slices will be especially delicious when baked. Beverages also basically cover all needs, soy milk, millet porridge and white fungus soup, coffee juice, black tea and yogurt. The children fell in love with all kinds of wheat circles and ate two bowls of soaked milk.
If you catch a plane and just want to make the most of your spare time, you might as well come here to experience it, it is very comfortable. come back next time.
